    Info

    Welcome to the generated API reference. Get Postman Collection

    Administración de Artista

    APIs para la gestion de artista

    Lista de la tabla artista.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "success": true,
    "data": {
        "current_page": 1,
        "data": [
            {
                "id": 2,
                "nombre": "Marcel",
                "manager": "Mauricio",
                "id_genero": 1
            },
            {
                "id": 3,
                "nombre": "MMM",
                "manager": "Mauricio",
                "id_genero": 1
            },
            {
                "id": 4,
                "nombre": "Marcel2",
                "manager": "Mauricio2",
                "id_genero": 1
            },
            {
                "id": 5,
                "nombre": "cinco",
                "manager": "Mauricio",
                "id_genero": 1
            }
        ],
        "first_page_url": "http:\/\/localhost\/api\/artista?page=1",
        "from": 1,
        "last_page": 1,
        "last_page_url": "http:\/\/localhost\/api\/artista?page=1",
        "next_page_url": null,
        "path": "http:\/\/localhost\/api\/artista",
        "per_page": 15,
        "prev_page_url": null,
        "to": 4,
        "total": 4
    },
    "message": "Artistas devueltos con éxito"
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/artista

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla artista

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    POST api/artista

    Lista un artista en especifico

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista/{artistum}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista/{artistum}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (404):

    {
    "success": false,
    "message": "Artista no encontrado"
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/artista/{artistum}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla artista

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista/{artistum}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista/{artistum}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/artista/{artistum}

    PATCH api/artista/{artistum}

    Elimina un elemento de la tabla artista

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista/{artistum}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/artista/{artistum}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/artista/{artistum}

    Listado de artistas por evento

    [Solo se mostrarán aquellos artistas que posean un evento asociado]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/listadoartistevento" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/listadoartistevento");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Administración de Auditorio

    APIs para la gestion de auditorio

    Lista de la tabla auditorio.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auditorio" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auditorio");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/auditorio

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla auditorio

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auditorio" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auditorio");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/auditorio/{auditorio}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla auditorio

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/auditorio/{auditorio}

    PATCH api/auditorio/{auditorio}

    Elimina un elemento de la tabla auditorio

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auditorio/{auditorio}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auditorio/{auditorio}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",

    HTTP Request

    GET api/listeventipo/{listeventipo}

    Detalle del evento

    [Se filtra por el ID del evento]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/detalle_evento/{detalle_evento}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/detalle_evento/{detalle_evento}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/detalle_evento/{detalle_evento}

    Buscar evento con filtros

    [Filtros por rango de precios, artista, tipo de evento. rango de fechas, (opcionales los parámetros de búsqueda)]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/buscar_evento" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/buscar_evento");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "precio_inicio": 100,
    "precio_fin": null,
    "artistas": [
        {
            "id_artist": 1
        },
        {
            "id_artist": 2
        }
    ],
    "tipos_evento": [
        {
            "id_tipo_evento": 1
        },
        {
            "id_tipo_evento": 2
        }
    ],
    "fecha_inicio": null,
    "fecha_fin": null
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/grupovendedorespto

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla grupovendedorespto

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupovendedorespto" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupovendedorespto");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/grupovendedorespto

    Lista los puntos de venta por grupo de vendedores en especifico

    [Se filtra por el ID del grupo del vendedor]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla grupovendedorespto

    [Se filtra por el ID del grupo del vendedor]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}

    PATCH api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}

    Elimina todos los elemento de la tabla grupovendedorespto

    [Se filtra por el ID del grupo del vendedor]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/grupovendedorespto/{grupovendedorespto}

    Administración de Grupos Vendedores

    APIs para la gestion de la tabla grups_vendedores

    Listado de los grupos de vendedores.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupsvendedore" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupsvendedore");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/grupsvendedore

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla grups_vendedores

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupsvendedore" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupsvendedore");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/grupsvendedore

    Lista un grupo de vendedor en especifico

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupsvendedore/{grupsvendedore}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupsvendedore/{grupsvendedore}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/grupsvendedore/{grupsvendedore}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla grups_vendedores

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupsvendedore/{grupsvendedore}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/grupsvendedore/{grupsvendedore}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/grupsvendedore/{grupsvendedore}

    PATCH api/grupsvendedore/{grupsvendedore}

})

    HTTP Request

    GET api/localidad

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla localidad

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/localidad" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/localidad");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "nombre": "Localidad New",
    "id_tribuna": 1,
    "puerta_acceso": null
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/localidad/{localidad}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla localidad

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/localidad/{localidad}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/localidad/{localidad}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "nombre": "Localidad 2",
    "id_tribuna": 1,
    "puerta_acceso": "AA12"
}

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/localidad/{localidad}

    PATCH api/localidad/{localidad}

    Elimina un elemento de la tabla localidad

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/localidad/{localidad}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/localidad/{localidad}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/localidad/{localidad}

    Administración de Palco

    APIs para la gestion de la tabla palco

    Lista de la tabla palco.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/palco" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/palco");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "success": true,
    "data": {
        "current_page": 1,
        "data": [
            {
                "id": 1,
                "nombre": "palco 1",
                "id_localidad": 1
            },
            {
                "id": 2,
                "nombre": "Palco 2",
                "id_localidad": 1
            },
            {
                "id": 3,
                "nombre": "Palco RR",
                "id_localidad": 1
            }
        ],
        "first_page_url": "http:\/\/localhost\/api\/palco?page=1",
        "from": 1,
        "last_page": 1,
        "last_page_url": "http:\/\/localhost\/api\/palco?page=1",
        "next_page_url": null,
        "path": "http:\/\/localhost\/api\/palco",
        "per_page": 15,
        "prev_page_url": null,
        "to": 3,
        "total": 3
    },
    "message": "Palcos devueltos con éxito"
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/palco

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla palco

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/palco" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/palco");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "nombre": "Palco New",
    "id_localidad": 1
}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/palco

    Lista de un palco en especifico

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/palco/{palco}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/palco/{palco}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "success": true,
    "data": {
        "id": 1,
        "nombre": "palco 1",
        "id_localidad": 1
    },
    "message": "Palco devuelto con éxito"
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/puesto

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla puesto

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puesto" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puesto");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "numero": "AA1",
    "id_localidad": 1,
    "id_fila": 1
}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/puesto

    Lista de una puesto en especifico

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puesto/{puesto}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puesto/{puesto}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/puesto/{puesto}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla puesto

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puesto/{puesto}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puesto/{puesto}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "numero": "BB1",
    "id_localidad": 1,
    "id_fila": 2
}

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/puesto/{puesto}

    PATCH api/puesto/{puesto}

    Elimina un elemento de la tabla puesto

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puesto/{puesto}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puesto/{puesto}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())

    Administración de Puestos - Palco

    Listado de los Puestos por Palcos.

    HTTP Request

    GET api/puestospalco

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla puestos_palco

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puestospalco" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puestospalco");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/puestospalco

    Lista de los puestos por palco en especifico

    [Se filtra por el ID del palco]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla puestos_palco

    [Se filtra por el ID del palco]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}

    PATCH api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}

    Elimina todos los elemento de la tabla puestos_palco

    [Se filtra por el ID del palco]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    DELETE api/puestospalco/{puestospalco}

    Administración de Punto de Venta Evento

    APIs para la gestion de la tabla puntoventa_evento

    Listado de los puntos de venta por evento.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventaevento" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventaevento");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/puntoventum

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla punto_venta

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventum" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventum");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/puntoventum

    Lista de un punto de venta en especifico

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla punto_venta

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}

    PATCH api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}

    Elimina un elemento de la tabla punto_venta

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/puntoventum/{puntoventum}

    Administración de Temporada

    APIs para la gestion de la tabla temporada

    Lista de la tabla temporada.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/temporada" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/temporada");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/tribuna

    Agrega un nuevo elemento a la tabla tribuna

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/tribuna" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/tribuna");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "nombre": "Tribuna Gold",
    "id_auditorio": 1
}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/tribuna

    Lista una tribuna en especifico

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/tribuna/{tribuna}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/tribuna/{tribuna}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/tribuna/{tribuna}

    Actualiza un elemeto de la tabla tribuna

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/tribuna/{tribuna}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/tribuna/{tribuna}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "nombre": "Tribuna Gold New",
    "id_auditorio": 2
}

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/tribuna/{tribuna}

    PATCH api/tribuna/{tribuna}

    Elimina un elemento de la tabla tribuna

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/tribuna/{tribuna}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/tribuna/{tribuna}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    Example request:

    HTTP Request

    GET api/listausuarios

    Compras realizadas por usuario

    [Se filtra por el ID del usuario]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/comprasrealizadas/{comprasrealizadas}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/comprasrealizadas/{comprasrealizadas}");

    "Accept": "application/json",

}

    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/comprasrealizadas/{comprasrealizadas}

    Temporadas compradas por usuario

    [Se filtra por el ID del usuario]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/temporadascompradas/{temporadascompradas}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/temporadascompradas/{temporadascompradas}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/temporadascompradas/{temporadascompradas}

    Reservas realizadas por usuario

    [Se filtra por el ID del usuario]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/reservas/{reservas}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/reservas/{reservas}");

    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/reservas/{reservas}

    Inicio de sesion del usuario

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/login" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/login");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "email": "email@example.com",
    "password": "1234567890"
}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/login

    Actualiza el perfil del usuario.

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/register" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/register");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/register

    Elimina un elemento de la tabla usuario

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/destroy" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/destroy");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/destroy

    Activar la cuenta del usuario

    [Se requiere Token enviado al correo]

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/signup/activate/{token}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/signup/activate/{token}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/signup/activate/{token}

    Redirigir al usuario a la página de autenticación de Google

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auth/{provider}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auth/{provider}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/auth/{provider}

    Obtener la información de usuario de Google.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auth/{provider}/callback" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/auth/{provider}/callback");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (429):

    {

    HTTP Request

    GET api/auth/{provider}/callback

    Cambio de clave del usuario.

    [El usuario debe estar logeado (Headers => Authorization => Bearer Token)]

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/cambioclave" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/cambioclave");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "mypassword": "Temporada Gold",
    "password": "1234567890",
    "c_password": "1234567890"
}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/cambioclave

    Detalles del usuario logeado

    [El usuario debe estar logeado (Headers => Authorization => Bearer Token)]

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/detailsuser" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/detailsuser");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    POST api/detailsuser

    Actualiza el perfil del usuario.

    [Se filtra por el ID]

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/updateprofile/{updateprofile}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/updateprofile/{updateprofile}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/updateprofile/{updateprofile}

    Cierre de sesion del usuario

    [Logout all devices] [El usuario debe estar logeado (Headers => Authorization => Bearer Token)]

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/logout" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/logout");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    POST api/logout

    Restablecimiento de contraseña

    APIs para la gestion del restablecimiento de la contraseña del usuario

    Creación del token para restablecer la contraseña

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/create" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/create");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "email": "email@example.com"
}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/create

    Buscar token para restablecer contraseña

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/find/{token}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/find/{token}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/find/{token}

    Restablecer la contraseña

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/reset" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/api/reset");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {}

    HTTP Request

    POST api/reset

    general

    Authorize a client to access the user's account.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/authorize" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/authorize");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET oauth/authorize

    Approve the authorization request.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/authorize" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/authorize");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    POST oauth/authorize

    Deny the authorization request.

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/authorize" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/authorize");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE oauth/authorize

    Authorize a client to access the user's account.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/token" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/token");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    POST oauth/token

    Get all of the authorized tokens for the authenticated user.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/tokens" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/tokens");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET oauth/tokens

    Delete the given token.

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/tokens/{token_id}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/tokens/{token_id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE oauth/tokens/{token_id}

    Get a fresh transient token cookie for the authenticated user.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/token/refresh" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/token/refresh");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    POST oauth/token/refresh

    Get all of the clients for the authenticated user.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/clients" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/clients");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET oauth/clients

    Store a new client.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/clients" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/clients");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    POST oauth/clients

    Update the given client.

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/clients/{client_id}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/clients/{client_id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    PUT oauth/clients/{client_id}

    Delete the given client.

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/clients/{client_id}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/clients/{client_id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE oauth/clients/{client_id}

    Get all of the available scopes for the application.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/scopes" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/scopes");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET oauth/scopes

    Get all of the personal access tokens for the authenticated user.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/personal-access-tokens" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/personal-access-tokens");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET oauth/personal-access-tokens

    Create a new personal access token for the user.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/personal-access-tokens" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/personal-access-tokens");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    POST oauth/personal-access-tokens

    Delete the given token.

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/personal-access-tokens/{token_id}" 
    const url = new URL("http://api.ticketshop.com.co/oauth/personal-access-tokens/{token_id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    DELETE oauth/personal-access-tokens/{token_id}

    bash javascript
